\"repo\": \"kubernetes/kubernetes\",\n      \"path\": \"staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"callHook\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The API server admission webhook chain in Kubernetes is implemented through a well-structured plugin architecture in the k8s.io/apiserver package. The chain consists of two main admission webhook types (MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook) with their respective dispatchers, configuration managers, and supporting infrastructure.\\n\\nExecution Flow:\\n1. The webhook admission controllers are registered as plugins (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go). These implement the admission.Interface with Admit() and Validate() methods respectively.\\n\\n2. When a request arrives, the plugin calls its Dispatch() method from the generic Webhook base class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go). The generic Webhook coordinates the overall admission process, including checking if the plugin is ready and retrieving the list of webhooks to call.\\n\\n3. For mutating webhooks, the flow proceeds through mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go), which iterates through each webhook in sequence. For validating webhooks, validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go) calls webhooks in parallel using goroutines.\\n\\n4. Key decision points include:\\n   - Namespace matching via predicates/namespace/matcher.go\\n   - Object selector matching via predicates/object/matcher.go  \\n   - Rule matching via predicates/rules/rules.go\\n   - CEL-based match conditions via matchconditions/matcher.go\\n   - These are coordinated through ShouldCallHook() in the generic webhook\\n\\n5. For each webhook that passes matching criteria:\\n   - Request/response objects are created (request/admissionreview.go) containing AdmissionReview objects\\n   - The webhook endpoint is called via REST client\\n   - For mutating webhooks, callAttrMutatingHook() processes the patch response and applies JSON patches to the object\\n   - For validating webhooks, callHook() validates the allowed/denied status\\n   - Responses are verified using VerifyAdmissionResponse() to ensure they conform to expected structure\\n\\n6. Webhook configuration is dynamically loaded via configuration managers:\\n   - MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager (configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go) discovers MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager (configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) discovers ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - Both use shared informers to stay synchronized with etcd\\n\\n7. Error handling and aggregation:\\n   - Mutating webhooks fail serially - first error terminates the chain\\n   - Validating webhooks aggregate multiple errors from parallel execution\\n   - Failure policies (Fail vs Ignore) determine whether to fail open or closed\\n   - Webhook timeout policies are enforced via context timeouts\\n\\nCore components:\\n- WebhookAccessor interface (accessors.go) provides a common abstraction for both mutating and validating webhook specifications\\n- Dispatcher interface defines the contract for dispatching webhook calls\\n- AdmissionResponse structure (request/admissionreview.go) holds webhook responses including patches, allowed status, and audit annotations\\n- Error types in errors/statuserror.go handle webhook-specific failures\\n\\nThis architecture enables dynamic, extensible admission control where webhook configurations can be added/removed at runtime without restarting the API server.\"\n}\nEOF\ncat /workspace/answer.json\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1678,"cache_read_input_tokens":57038,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1678},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6ed76636-742a-4f8f-a954-d67f7aecdff2","uuid":"a3288bf8-0a69-4c73-9f28-8862e347d58c"}

\"The API server admission webhook chain in Kubernetes is implemented through a well-structured plugin architecture in the k8s.io/apiserver package. The chain consists of two main admission webhook types (MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook) with their respective dispatchers, configuration managers, and supporting infrastructure.\\n\\nExecution Flow:\\n1. The webhook admission controllers are registered as plugins (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go). These implement the admission.Interface with Admit() and Validate() methods respectively.\\n\\n2. When a request arrives, the plugin calls its Dispatch() method from the generic Webhook base class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go). The generic Webhook coordinates the overall admission process, including checking if the plugin is ready and retrieving the list of webhooks to call.\\n\\n3. For mutating webhooks, the flow proceeds through mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go), which iterates through each webhook in sequence. For validating webhooks, validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go) calls webhooks in parallel using goroutines.\\n\\n4. Key decision points include:\\n   - Namespace matching via predicates/namespace/matcher.go\\n   - Object selector matching via predicates/object/matcher.go  \\n   - Rule matching via predicates/rules/rules.go\\n   - CEL-based match conditions via matchconditions/matcher.go\\n   - These are coordinated through ShouldCallHook() in the generic webhook\\n\\n5. For each webhook that passes matching criteria:\\n   - Request/response objects are created (request/admissionreview.go) containing AdmissionReview objects\\n   - The webhook endpoint is called via REST client\\n   - For mutating webhooks, callAttrMutatingHook() processes the patch response and applies JSON patches to the object\\n   - For validating webhooks, callHook() validates the allowed/denied status\\n   - Responses are verified using VerifyAdmissionResponse() to ensure they conform to expected structure\\n\\n6. Webhook configuration is dynamically loaded via configuration managers:\\n   - MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager (configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go) discovers MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager (configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) discovers ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - Both use shared informers to stay synchronized with etcd\\n\\n7. Error handling and aggregation:\\n   - Mutating webhooks fail serially - first error terminates the chain\\n   - Validating webhooks aggregate multiple errors from parallel execution\\n   - Failure policies (Fail vs Ignore) determine whether to fail open or closed\\n   - Webhook timeout policies are enforced via context timeouts\\n\\nCore components:\\n- WebhookAccessor interface (accessors.go) provides a common abstraction for both mutating and validating webhook specifications\\n- Dispatcher interface defines the contract for dispatching webhook calls\\n- AdmissionResponse structure (request/admissionreview.go) holds webhook responses including patches, allowed status, and audit annotations\\n- Error types in errors/statuserror.go handle webhook-specific failures\\n\\nThis \"The API server admission webhook chain in Kubernetes is implemented through a well-structured plugin architecture in the k8s.io/apiserver package. The chain consists of two main admission webhook types (MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook) with their respective dispatchers, configuration managers, and supporting infrastructure.\\n\\nExecution Flow:\\n1. The webhook admission controllers are registered as plugins (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and validating/plugin.go). These implement the admission.Interface with Admit() and Validate() methods respectively.\\n\\n2. When a request arrives, the plugin calls its Dispatch() method from the generic Webhook base class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go). The generic Webhook coordinates the overall admission process, including checking if the plugin is ready and retrieving the list of webhooks to call.\\n\\n3. For mutating webhooks, the flow proceeds through mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go), which iterates through each webhook in sequence. For validating webhooks, validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go) calls webhooks in parallel using goroutines.\\n\\n4. Key decision points include:\\n   - Namespace matching via predicates/namespace/matcher.go\\n   - Object selector matching via predicates/object/matcher.go  \\n   - Rule matching via predicates/rules/rules.go\\n   - CEL-based match conditions via matchconditions/matcher.go\\n   - These are coordinated through ShouldCallHook() in the generic webhook\\n\\n5. For each webhook that passes matching criteria:\\n   - Request/response objects are created (request/admissionreview.go) containing AdmissionReview objects\\n   - The webhook endpoint is called via REST client\\n   - For mutating webhooks, callAttrMutatingHook() processes the patch response and applies JSON patches to the object\\n   - For validating webhooks, callHook() validates the allowed/denied status\\n   - Responses are verified using VerifyAdmissionResponse() to ensure they conform to expected structure\\n\\n6. Webhook configuration is dynamically loaded via configuration managers:\\n   - MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager (configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go) discovers MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager (configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) discovers ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - Both use shared informers to stay synchronized with etcd\\n\\n7. Error handling and aggregation:\\n   - Mutating webhooks fail serially - first error terminates the chain\\n   - Validating webhooks aggregate multiple errors from parallel execution\\n   - Failure policies (Fail vs Ignore) determine whether to fail open or closed\\n   - Webhook timeout policies are enforced via context timeouts\\n\\nCore components:\\n- WebhookAccessor interface (accessors.go) provides a common abstraction for both mutating and validating webhook specifications\\n- Dispatcher interface defines the contract for dispatching webhook calls\\n- AdmissionResponse structure (request/admissionreview.go) holds webhook responses including patches, allowed status, and audit annotations\\n- Error types in errors/statuserror.go handle webhook-specific failures\\n\\nThis architecture enables dynamic, extensible admission control where webhook configurations can be added/removed at runtime without restarting the API server.\"\n}","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
